negotiating rates with your potential clients seems like one of the most complex or intimidating parts of freelancing. But, it does not have to be! WEAR YOUR DETECTIVE LENSES The first step is to do your homework. Detectives and investigators compile evidences through careful observations and interviewing witnesses. Play the role of a “detective” by collecting as many salary information as you can.
